SELECT COUNT(*) FROM company_name AS cn1, info_type AS it2, kind_type AS kt1, kind_type AS kt2, link_type AS lt, movie_companies AS mc1, movie_companies AS mc2, movie_info_idx AS mi_idx2, movie_link AS ml, title AS t1, title AS t2 WHERE cn1.country_code = '[nl]' AND it2.info = 'rating' AND kt1.kind IN ('tv series') AND kt2.kind IN ('tv series') AND lt.link LIKE '%follow%' AND mi_idx2.info < '3.0' AND t2.production_year = 2007 AND cn1.id = mc1.company_id AND it2.id = mi_idx2.info_type_id AND kt1.id = t1.kind_id AND kt2.id = t2.kind_id AND lt.id = ml.link_type_id AND mi_idx2.movie_id = mc2.movie_id AND ml.linked_movie_id = mc2.movie_id AND ml.movie_id = mc1.movie_id AND t1.id = mc1.movie_id AND t2.id = mc2.movie_id;#####4.0
SELECT COUNT(*) FROM company_name AS cn1, company_name AS cn2, info_type AS it2, kind_type AS kt1, kind_type AS kt2, link_type AS lt, movie_companies AS mc1, movie_companies AS mc2, movie_info_idx AS mi_idx2, movie_link AS ml, title AS t1, title AS t2 WHERE cn1.country_code = '[nl]' AND it2.info = 'rating' AND kt1.kind IN ('tv series') AND kt2.kind IN ('tv series') AND lt.link LIKE '%follow%' AND mi_idx2.info < '3.0' AND t2.production_year = 2007 AND cn1.id = mc1.company_id AND cn2.id = mc2.company_id AND it2.id = mi_idx2.info_type_id AND kt1.id = t1.kind_id AND kt2.id = t2.kind_id AND lt.id = ml.link_type_id AND mi_idx2.movie_id = mc2.movie_id AND ml.linked_movie_id = mc2.movie_id AND ml.movie_id = mc1.movie_id AND t1.id = mc1.movie_id AND t2.id = mc2.movie_id;#####4.0
